(*****************************************************************

 The category of pointed posets and strict functions

 We construct the category of pointed posets and strict monotone
 functions as a category of structured sets. In addition, we show
 that this category is monoidal closed via the smash product.

 Contents
 1. Structures of pointed posets
 2. The cartesian structure of pointed posets
 3. Limits of pointed posets
 4. Pointed posets form a pointed structure
 5. The smash product of pointed posets

 *****************************************************************)

Notation "_ ≠ _" was already used in scope nat_scope.
[notation-overridden,parsing,default]

Definition struct_pointed_poset_strict
  : hset_struct
  := struct_pointed_poset_strict_data ,, struct_pointed_poset_strict_laws.

Definition category_of_pointed_poset_strict
  : category
  := category_of_hset_struct struct_pointed_poset_strict.

         apply is_strict_and_monotone_depfunction_pointed_poset_pair ;
         exact Hfs).

(**
 4. Pointed posets form a pointed structure
 *)
Definition pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict_data
  : pointed_hset_struct_data struct_pointed_poset_strict
  := λ X RX, ⊥_{RX}.

X, Y: hSet
RX: struct_pointed_poset_strict X
RY: struct_pointed_poset_strict Y
mor_hset_struct struct_pointed_poset_strict RX RY
  (λ _ : X,
   hset_struct_point
     pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict_data RY)

    apply constant_is_strict_and_monotone.
  
∏ (X Y : hSet) (f : X → Y)
(PX : struct_pointed_poset_strict X)
(PY : struct_pointed_poset_strict Y),
mor_hset_struct struct_pointed_poset_strict PX PY f
→ f
    (hset_struct_point
       pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict_data PX) =
  hset_struct_point
    pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict_data PY
 
X, Y: hSet
f: X → Y
PX: pointed_PartialOrder X
PY: pointed_PartialOrder Y
Pf: is_strict_and_monotone PX PY f
f
  (hset_struct_point
     pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict_data PX) =
hset_struct_point
  pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict_data PY

    apply Pf.
Qed.

Definition pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict
  : pointed_hset_struct struct_pointed_poset_strict
  := pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict_data
     ,,
     pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict_laws.

(**
 5. The smash product of pointed posets
 *)

X, Y: hSet
PX: pointed_PartialOrder X
PY: pointed_PartialOrder Y
xy₁, xy₂: X × Y
smash_eqrel cartesian_struct_pointed_poset_strict
  pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict PX PY xy₁ xy₂ <->
downward_closed_to_eqrel (smash_set PX PY) xy₁ xy₂

  pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict PX PY xy₁ xy₂ <->
downward_closed_to_eqrel (smash_set PX PY) xy₁ xy₂

  pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict PX PY (x₁,, y₁)
  xy₂ <->
downward_closed_to_eqrel (smash_set PX PY) (x₁,, y₁)
  xy₂

  (downward_closed_to_eqrel (smash_set PX PY)

    (x₂,, y₂)

x₁: X
y₁: Y
x₂: X
y₂: Y
p: (x₁,, y₁ = x₂,, y₂)
⨿ ((pr1 (x₁,, y₁) =
    hset_struct_point
      pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict PX)
   ⨿ (pr2 (x₁,, y₁) =
      hset_struct_point
        pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict PY)
   × (pr1 (x₂,, y₂) =
      hset_struct_point
        pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict PX)
     ⨿ (pr2 (x₂,, y₂) =
        hset_struct_point
          pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict PY))
downward_closed_to_eqrel (smash_set PX PY) (x₁,, y₁)
  (x₂,, y₂)

x₁: X
y₁: Y
x₂: X
y₂: Y
p: (x₁,, y₁ = x₂,, y₂)
⨿ ((x₁ =
    pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict_data X PX)
   ⨿ (y₁ =
      pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict_data Y
        PY)
   × (x₂ =
      pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict_data X
        PX)
     ⨿ (y₂ =
        pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict_data Y
          PY))
downward_closed_to_eqrel (smash_set PX PY) (x₁,, y₁)
  (x₂,, y₂)

y₁: Y
x₂: X
y₂: Y

⨿ ((x₁ = ⊥_{ PX}) ⨿ (y₁ = ⊥_{ PY})
   × (x₂ = ⊥_{ PX}) ⨿ (y₂ = ⊥_{ PY}))
downward_closed_to_eqrel (smash_set PX PY) (x₁,, y₁)
  (x₂,, y₂)

y₂: Y

   × (x₂ = ⊥_{ PX}) ⨿ (y₂ = ⊥_{ PY}))
(x₁,, y₁ = x₂,, y₂)%logic
⨿ (smash_set PX PY (x₁,, y₁)
   ∧ smash_set PX PY (x₂,, y₂))

  pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict PX PY (x₁,, y₁)

× ishinh_UU ((x₂ = ⊥_{ PX}) ⨿ (y₂ = ⊥_{ PY}))
p₁: (x₁ = ⊥_{ PX}) ⨿ (y₁ = ⊥_{ PY})
p₂: (λ _ : ishinh_UU
         ((x₁ = ⊥_{ PX}) ⨿ (y₁ = ⊥_{ PY})),
 ishinh_UU ((x₂ = ⊥_{ PX}) ⨿ (y₂ = ⊥_{ PY})))
  (pr1 p)

  pointed_struct_pointed_poset_strict PX PY (x₁,, y₁)
  (x₂,, y₂)

∏
(PX PY
 PZ : category_of_hset_struct
        cartesian_struct_pointed_poset_strict)
(f : category_of_hset_struct
       cartesian_struct_pointed_poset_strict
     ⟦ hset_struct_with_smash_setquot_ob
         struct_pointed_poset_strict_with_smash PX PY,
     PZ ⟧),
mor_hset_struct cartesian_struct_pointed_poset_strict
  (pr2 PX)
  (pr1
     struct_pointed_poset_strict_with_smash_closed_pointed
     (pr1 PY) (pr1 PZ) (pr2 PY) (pr2 PZ))
  (hset_struct_smash_uncurry_fun
     struct_pointed_poset_strict_with_smash f)
 
PX, PY, PZ: category_of_hset_struct
  cartesian_struct_pointed_poset_strict
f: category_of_hset_struct
  cartesian_struct_pointed_poset_strict
⟦ hset_struct_with_smash_setquot_ob
    struct_pointed_poset_strict_with_smash PX PY,
PZ ⟧
mor_hset_struct cartesian_struct_pointed_poset_strict
